                    <div class="photo-of-day-info">
                        <a class="photo-of-day-title">Ugašen olimpijski plamen u Italiji: Norveška najuspešnija u Milanu i Kortini</a>
                        <p class="photo-of-day-desc">Zimske olimpijske igre u Milanu i Kortini svečano su zatvorene u ceremonijom pod sloganom &quot;Lepota u akciji&quot;, uz bogat umetnički program i defile sportista. Predsednica Međunarodnog olimpijskog komiteta Kirsti Koventri zvanično je proglasila kraj Igara i pozvala svet na novo okupljanje 2030. godine u francuskim Alpima, nakon čega je ugašen olimpijski plamen. Olimpijska zastava predata je predstavnicima budućih domaćina, čime je simbolično započeto novo poglavlje pod nazivom &quot;Nova zora&quot;.</p>

<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/raphael/2.2.7/raphael.min.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
<script src="/files/js/jquery.mapael.js?t=24-13-59" type="text/javascript"></script>
<script src="/files/js/map/european_union.js?t=24-13-59" type="text/javascript"></script>

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function() {
                    var pollId = "13";
                    var storageKey = "Arena sport TV - moj trenutak, moj teren, moja tribina - Arena Sport TV" + '_' + 'survey_vote' + '_' + pollId;
                    let pollDateTo = "2026-02-26"
                    let date = new Date(); // TRENUTNI DATUM
                    let currentDate = date.getFullYear() + "-" + ("0" + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "-" + ("0" + (date.getDate() + 1)).slice(-2); // FORMIRAN DATUM 'Y-m-d'

                    if(!(localStorage.getItem(storageKey)) && (pollDateTo >= currentDate)){
                        showForm();
                    }else {
                        showResults();
                    }
                    function showForm() {
                        $.ajax({
                        url: "https://www.tvarenasport.com/ajax/get-poll-answers-form-for-poll-page",
                        type: "post",
                        "data": {
                            '_token': '',
                            'pollId':"13",
                        }
                        }).done(function(response) {
                            $('.survey-anketa-widget .survey-inner').html(response)

                            $('.survey-anketa-widget #vote').on('click',function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                $.ajax({
                                    url: "https://www.tvarenasport.com/ajax/poll-page-answer-vote",
                                    type: "post",
                                    "data": {
                                        '_token': '',
                                        'answer':$('#answers:checked').val(),
                                        'pollId':"13"
                                    }
                                }).done(function(r) {
                                    $('.survey-anketa-widget .survey-inner').html(r);
                                    localStorage.setItem(storageKey, true);

                                })

                            });

                            $('.survey-anketa-widget #results').on('click',function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                showResults();
                            })
                            $('.survey-anketa-widget #vote_page').removeClass('d-none');
                        })
                    }

                function showResults() {
                    $.ajax({
                        url: "https://www.tvarenasport.com/ajax/get-poll-results-form-for-poll-page",
                        type: "post",
                        "data": {
                            '_token': '',
                            'pollId':"13",
                            'result':true
                                    }
                        }).done(function(r) {
                            $('.survey-anketa-widget .survey-inner').html(r);
                            $('.survey-anketa-widget #vote_page').on('click',function(e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    showForm();
                            })

                            if(!(localStorage.getItem(storageKey)) && (pollDateTo >= currentDate)){
                                $('.survey-anketa-widget #vote_page').removeClass('d-none');
                            }else {
                                $('.survey-anketa-widget #vote_page').addClass('d-none');
                            }

                        })
                }
            })

        </script>
        <script>
        $(document).ready(function(){
            $('.yt-video-link').on('click',function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                let videoID = $(this).data('video-id');
                $('#yt-video-iframe').attr("src", "https://www.youtube.com/embed/"+videoID);
            });

            $('#close-yt-modal').on('click',function(){
                $('#yt-video-iframe').attr("src", "");
            })
        });
    </script>
